  f1r  [text]
============================================================
  EVA: fachys ykal ar ataiin shol shory cthres y kor sholdy
  ITA: nseail mits ei deiti moen seoen npeeta s eot srmoen

  EVA: sory ckhar or y kair chtaiin shar are cthar cthar dan
  ITA: seon eieta eo s erit deitea eien pei eieta eieta dir

  EVA: syaiir sheky or ykaiin shod cthoary cthes daraiin sa
  ITA: eeisn stpen eo deits roen seioeta npeta deieir in

  EVA: ooiin oteey oteos roloty cthar daiin otaiin or okan
  ITA: deoo sppto nopto stomoe eieta deir deito eo dito

  EVA: dair y chear cthaiin cphar cfhaiin
  ITA: erir s eipea deieta eiela deiela

  EVA: ydaraishy
  ITA: senrieirs

  EVA: odar o y shol cphoy oydar sh s cfhoaiin shodary
  ITA: eiro o s moen soela eirso en n deioela seiroen

  EVA: yshey shody okchoy otchol chocthy oschy dain chor kos
  ITA: spens sroen soeato moeato setaoea seano drir eoea not

  EVA: daiin shos cfhol shody
  ITA: deir noen moela sroen

  EVA: dain os teody
  ITA: drir no sropt

  EVA: ydain cphesaiin ol s cphey ytain shoshy cphodales
  ITA: drirs deinpela mo n spela drits senoen npmiroela

  EVA: oksho kshoy otairin oteol okan shodain sckhey daiin
  ITA: oento soent drerito mopto dito driroen spetan deir

  EVA: shoy ckhey kodaiin cphy cphodaiils cthey she oldain d
  ITA: soen speta deirot sela nmeiroela speta pen drirmo r

  EVA: dain oiin chol odaiin chodain chdy okain dan cthy kod
  ITA: drir deo moea deiro driroea srea drito dir seta rot

  EVA: daiin shckhey ckeor chor shey kol chol chol kor chal
  ITA: deir spetaen eopta eoea spen mot moea moea eot miea

  EVA: sho chol shodan kshy kchy dor chodaiin sho kchom
  ITA: oen moea diroen sent seat eor deiroea oen goeat

  EVA: ycho tchey chokain sheo pshol dydyd cthy daicthy
  ITA: oeas speat dritoea open moenl rsrsr seta setarir

  EVA: yto shol she kodshey cphealy dasain dain ckhyds
  ITA: ots moen pen spenrot smipela drinir drir nrseta

  EVA: dchar shcthaiin okaiir chey rchy potol cthols dlocta
  ITA: eiear deietaen eeito spea seae motol nmoeta itaomr

  EVA: shok chor chey dain ckhey
  ITA: toen eoea spea drir speta

  EVA: otol daiiin
  ITA: moto dreir

  EVA: cpho shaiin shokcheey chol tshodeesy shey pydeey chy ro d
  ITA: oela deien sppeatoen moea snpproent spen spprsl sea oe r

  EVA: doin chol dain cthal dar shear kaiin dar shey cthar
  ITA: dror moea drir mieta eir eipen deit eir spen eieta

  EVA: choo kaiin shoaiin okol daiin far cthol daiin ctholdar
  ITA: ooea deit deioen moto deir eil moeta deir eirmoeta

  EVA: ycheey okay oky daiin okchey kokaiin chol kchy dal
  ITA: sppeas sito sto deir speato deitot moea seat mir

  EVA: deeo shody koshey cthy okchey keey keey dal chtor

  EVA: eo chol chok choty chotey
  ITA: op moea toea stoea sptoea

  EVA: dchaiin
  ITA: deiear
